POUs
----


F_CalculateAbsorptionConstant
^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^

::

    (*
    This calculates the mass attenuation coefficient mu.

    The mass absorption coefficient is proportional to the atomic
    photoabsorption cross-section by Avagadros number $N_A$ and atomic weight $A$.

    $$\mu_m = \frac{N_A}{A} \sigma_a$$

    Ref: http://xdb.lbl.gov/Section1/Sec_1-6.pdf

    The atomic photoabsorption cross-section for an element is dependant on the
    photon wavelength $\lambda$ and the energy-specific atomic scattering factor $f_2$

    $$ \sigma_a = 2 r_0 \lambda f_2 $$

    http://henke.lbl.gov/optical_constants/intro.html

    Using chosen values for the material constants, the transmission can be
     expressed in terms of the photon wavelength and corresponding atomic scattering factor $f_2$,

    $$ T = \frac{I}{I_0} = e^{-\mu d} = e^{-2 r_0 \lambda f_2 \frac{N_A}{A}\rho d}$$
    *)
    FUNCTION F_CalculateAbsorptionConstant : LREAL
    VAR_INPUT
        sElement : STRING;
        fEnergyEV: LREAL;
        fDensity_gm3 : LREAL; (* Density in g m^-3 *)
        fAtomicWeight: LREAL;
    END_VAR
    VAR
        f2 : LREAL;
    END_VAR
    VAR_OUTPUT
        (* Access by way of F_CalculateAbsorptionConstant(..., bError => bError); *)
        bError : BOOL;
    END_VAR
    VAR CONSTANT
        NA : LREAL := GVL_PhysicalConstants.fAvogadroConstant_in_mol_1;
        r0 : LREAL := GVL_PhysicalConstants.fClassicalElectronRadius_in_m;
        h  : LREAL := GVL_PhysicalConstants.fPlanckConstantInEV_Hz_in_eV_Hz_1;
        c  : LREAL := GVL_PhysicalConstants.fSpeedOfLightInVacuum_in_m_s_1;
    END_VAR
    (*

    Python reference code:

        NA = scipy.constants.Avogadro
        c = scipy.constants.speed_of_light
        h, *_ = scipy.constants.physical_constants['Planck constant in eV/Hz']
        r0, *_ = scipy.constants.physical_constants['classical electron radius']

        # The absorption constant:
        mu = ((2 * r0 * h * c * fs/eV_space) * density *
              (NA / atomic_weight))

    *)
    fbScatteringFactorLUT(
        sTableName:=sElement,
        fEnergyEV:=fEnergyEV,
        bError=>bError,
    );

    IF bError THEN
        RETURN;
    END_IF

    f2 := fbScatteringFactorLUT.f2;

    F_CalculateAbsorptionConstant := (
        (2.0 * r0 * h * c * f2 / fEnergyEV) *
        fDensity_gm3 * (NA / fAtomicWeight)
    );

    END_FUNCTION


Related:
    * `GVL_PhysicalConstants`_


F_CalculateTransmission
^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^

::

    FUNCTION F_CalculateTransmission : LREAL
    VAR_INPUT
        fAbsorptionConstant : LREAL; (* The absorption constant mu, calculated by F_CalculateAbsorptionConstant *)
        fThickness_in_m : LREAL; (* Thickness of the material [m] *)
    END_VAR
    F_CalculateTransmission := EXP(-fAbsorptionConstant * fThickness_in_m);

    END_FUNCTION


Related:
    * `F_CalculateAbsorptionConstant`_

        sDescription := 'Atomic number of Og (oganesson)';

    ELSE
        bFound := FALSE;
        nValue := -1;

    END_IF

    END_FUNCTION_BLOCK




FB_AtomicNumber_Test
^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^

::

    FUNCTION_BLOCK FB_AtomicNumber_Test EXTENDS TcUnit.FB_TestSuite
    VAR
        nTestID : INT;
        fbAtomicNumber : FB_AtomicNumber;
    END_VAR
    nTestID := 0;

    TestInvalidElementExpectNotFoundAndNegativeAtomicNumber(
        sName := 'INVALID'
    );

    TestValidElementExpectFoundAndCorrectAtomicNumber(
        sName := 'Be',
        nExpectedNumber := 4
    );

    TestValidElementExpectFoundAndCorrectAtomicNumber(
        sName := 'H',
        nExpectedNumber := 1
    );

    TestValidElementExpectFoundAndCorrectAtomicNumber(
        sName := 'Ca',
        nExpectedNumber := 20
    );

    TestValidElementExpectFoundAndCorrectAtomicNumber(
        sName := 'Lr',
        nExpectedNumber := 103
    );

    TestValidElementExpectFoundAndCorrectAtomicNumber(
        sName := 'Nb',
        nExpectedNumber := 41
    );

    END_FUNCTION_BLOCK

    METHOD TestInvalidElementExpectNotFoundAndNegativeAtomicNumber
    VAR_INPUT
        sName : STRING;
    END_VAR
    TEST(CONCAT('TestInvalidElementExpectNotFoundAndNegativeAtomicNumber ID: ',
        INT_TO_STRING(nTestID))
    );

    fbAtomicNumber(
        sName := sName,
        bFound =>,
        nValue =>,
    );

    AssertFalse(
        Condition := fbAtomicNumber.bFound,
        Message := 'Expected bFound bit to be false but it was true.'
    );

    AssertTrue(
        Condition := fbAtomicNumber.nValue < 0,
        Message := CONCAT('Expected atomic number to be negative but it was [',
            CONCAT(INT_TO_STRING(fbAtomicNumber.nValue),
            '].'))
    );

    TEST_FINISHED();

    nTestID := nTestID + 1;
    END_METHOD

    METHOD TestValidElementExpectFoundAndCorrectAtomicNumber
    VAR_INPUT
        sName : STRING;
        nExpectedNumber : INT;
    END_VAR
    TEST(CONCAT('TestValidElementExpectFoundAndCorrectAtomicNumber ID: ',
        INT_TO_STRING(nTestID))
    );

    fbAtomicNumber(
        sName := sName,
        bFound =>,
        nValue =>,
    );

    AssertTrue(
        Condition := fbAtomicNumber.bFound,
        Message := 'Expected bFound bit to be true but it was false.'
    );

    AssertEquals_INT(
        Expected := nExpectedNumber,
        Actual := fbAtomicNumber.nValue,
        Message := CONCAT('Expected atomic number to be [',
            CONCAT(INT_TO_STRING(nExpectedNumber),
            CONCAT('] but it was [',
            CONCAT(INT_TO_STRING(fbAtomicNumber.nValue),
            ']'))))
    );

    TEST_FINISHED();

    nTestID := nTestID + 1;
    END_METHOD

        bInit := TRUE;
    END_IF

    (* Get correct table *)


    IF sTableName = 'Ge' THEN
        iRowSize := ADR(fTable_Ge[1,0]) - ADR(fTable_Ge[0,0]);
        iRowCount := 505;
        fRow1 := ADR(fTable_Ge[0, 0]);
        fTableLookupLow := 10.0000;
        fTableLookupHigh := 30000.0;
    ELSIF sTableName = 'C' THEN
        iRowSize := ADR(fTable_C[1,0]) - ADR(fTable_C[0,0]);
        iRowCount := 501;
        fRow1 := ADR(fTable_C[0, 0]);
        fTableLookupLow := 10.0000;
        fTableLookupHigh := 30000.0;
    ELSIF sTableName = 'Al' THEN
        iRowSize := ADR(fTable_Al[1,0]) - ADR(fTable_Al[0,0]);
        iRowCount := 503;
        fRow1 := ADR(fTable_Al[0, 0]);
        fTableLookupLow := 10.0000;
        fTableLookupHigh := 30000.0;
    ELSIF sTableName = 'Be' THEN
        iRowSize := ADR(fTable_Be[1,0]) - ADR(fTable_Be[0,0]);
        iRowCount := 723;
        fRow1 := ADR(fTable_Be[0, 0]);
        fTableLookupLow := 10.0000;
        fTableLookupHigh := 30000.0;
    ELSIF sTableName = 'Si' THEN
        iRowSize := ADR(fTable_Si[1,0]) - ADR(fTable_Si[0,0]);
        iRowCount := 755;
        fRow1 := ADR(fTable_Si[0, 0]);
        fTableLookupLow := 10.0000;
        fTableLookupHigh := 30000.0;
    ELSE
        bError := TRUE;
        bDone := TRUE;
        RETURN;
    END_IF

    IF fEnergyEV < fTableLookupLow THEN
        bDone := TRUE;
        RETURN;
    ELSIF fEnergyEV > fTableLookupHigh THEN
        bDone := TRUE;
        RETURN;
    END_IF

    FOR iRowIdx := 0 TO iRowCount - 1
    DO
        fRow2 := fRow1 + iRowSize;
        IF fEnergyEV >= fRow1^[0] AND fEnergyEV <= fRow2^[0] THEN
            fEnergyEV_RowDelta := fRow2^[0] - fRow1^[0];
            IF fEnergyEV_RowDelta <= 0.0 THEN
                bFound := TRUE;
                bError := TRUE;
                bDone := TRUE;
            ELSE

                // Interpolate output: f1
                fSlope := (fRow2^[1] - fRow1^[1]) / fEnergyEV_RowDelta;
                f1 := fRow1^[1] + fSlope * (fEnergyEV - fRow1^[0]);

                // Interpolate output: f2
                fSlope := (fRow2^[2] - fRow1^[2]) / fEnergyEV_RowDelta;
                f2 := fRow1^[2] + fSlope * (fEnergyEV - fRow1^[0]);

                bFound := TRUE;
                bError := FALSE;
                bDone := TRUE;
            END_IF
            RETURN;
        END_IF
        fRow1 := fRow2;
    END_FOR

    END_FUNCTION_BLOCK

FB_TestElementDensity
^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^

::

    FUNCTION_BLOCK FB_TestElementDensity EXTENDS TcUnit.FB_TestSuite
    VAR
        fbElementDensity : FB_ElementDensity;
    END_VAR
    TEST('fbElementDensity Si lookup');

    fbElementDensity(sName:='Si');
    AssertTrue(fbElementDensity.bFound, 'Silicon not found');
    AssertEquals_LREAL(2.33, fbElementDensity.fValue, Delta:=0.0001, Message:='Element density constant value');
    TEST_FINISHED();

    TEST('fbElementDensity bad name lookup');
    fbElementDensity(sName:='Silicon');
    AssertFalse(fbElementDensity.bFound, 'Silicon should not be found');
    AssertEquals_LREAL(0.0, fbElementDensity.fValue, Delta:=0.0001, Message:='Element density constant value');
    TEST_FINISHED();

    END_FUNCTION_BLOCK


Related:
    * `FB_ElementDensity`_


FB_TestTransmission
^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^

::

    FUNCTION_BLOCK FB_TestTransmission EXTENDS TcUnit.FB_TestSuite
    VAR_INPUT
    END_VAR
    VAR_OUTPUT
    END_VAR
    VAR
        fMu: LREAL;
        bError: BOOL;
        fTransmission: LREAL;
    END_VAR
    TEST('Absorption constant');


    (* Cherry-picked test values, verified by Python solid-attenuator IOC *)
    fMu := F_CalculateAbsorptionConstant(
        sElement:='C',
        fEnergyEV:=10000,
        fDensity_gm3:=3.51E6,  (* C (Diamond) g/m^3 *)
        fAtomicWeight:=12.0107,
        bError=>bError,
    );
    AssertFalse(bError, 'F_CalculateAbsorptionConstant lookup reported error');
    AssertEquals_LREAL(724.7224642932565, fMu, Delta:=0.0001, Message:='Absorption constant value');
    TEST_FINISHED();

    TEST('F_CalculateTransmission');
    fTransmission := F_CalculateTransmission(fAbsorptionConstant:=fMu, fThickness_in_m:=1E-3);
    AssertEquals_LREAL(0.4844590049714352, fTransmission, Delta:=0.0001, Message:='Transmission check');
    TEST_FINISHED();

    END_FUNCTION_BLOCK


Related:
    * `F_CalculateAbsorptionConstant`_
    * `F_CalculateTransmission`_


RunTests
^^^^^^^^

::

    PROGRAM RunTests
    VAR
        fbScatteringFactorLUT_Test : FB_ScatteringFactorLUT_Test;
        fbTestTransmission : FB_TestTransmission;
        fbTestElementDensity : FB_TestElementDensity;
        fbAtomicNumber_Test : FB_AtomicNumber_Test;

        (* Smoke test - just instantiate *)
        fbPhysicalConstants : FB_PhysicalConstants;
        fbAtomicMass : FB_AtomicMass;

    END_VAR
    TcUnit.RUN();

    fbPhysicalConstants();
    fbAtomicMass();

    END_PROGRAM
